  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

  <span id="freeText10873106849112878664" style="display:none"><i>History is on repeat, and things didn't go so well the last time.</i><br /><br />Alexandria isn't sure she's going to make it to her eighteenth birthday--to her Awakening. A long-forgotten, fanatical order is out to kill her, and if the Council ever discovers what she did in the Catskills, she's a goner... and so is Aiden.<br /><br />If that's not freaky enough, whenever Alex and Seth spend time "training"--which really is just Seth's code word for some up-close and personal one-on-one time--she ends up with another mark of the Apollyon, which brings her one step closer to Awakening ahead of schedule. Awesome. <br /><br />But as her birthday draws near, her entire world shatters with a startling revelation and she's caught between love and Fate. One will do anything to protect her. One has been lying to her since the beginning. Once the gods have revealed themselves, unleashing their wrath, lives will be irrevocably changed... and destroyed.<br /><br />Those left standing will discover if love is truly greater than Fate...</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11721627099384961539">04/11/2012<br/>Just read the book... OMG!! I was going crazy reading it and the end... The end!!   <span id="freeText14723998478656252629" style="display:none">50 gazillion million trillion stars! This book was AMAZING. I have never read a book that has kept me excited as this<a href="http://s624.photobucket.com/albums/tt322/atx_shawty2009/?action=view&amp;current=ExcitedKitty.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379774378i/328422.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yes, this cat sums up ALL of my emotions while reading this book!<br><br><br>This will be a quick an short review since this is an ARC. I will try not to give too much spoilers I PROMISE! I don't want any death threats in my email lol.<br><br><br>The story start where we left off in book 2 Alex is taken back to the covenant as you all know and well, after everything that has happened Alex, is basically on LOCK DOWN until her eighteenth birthday in which she does not want to come. In the begenning Alex finds out some shocking news about her father that you are just going to have to read to find out! Book three is full of so many twist, turns and surprises that is going to have you saying "OH MY GOD'S!" throughout the whole book!<br><br><br><b>Alex:</b> Is still her kick/smart ass self and just can't seem to catch a break in this book. Alex is put through the ultimate test when it comes to her fate and what she feels is right. Alex has to make a life changing decision that can put the people she loves in a life threatening situation. <br><br>I really loved Alex and felt like I connected more with her on an emotional level. Yes, Alex can Irrational and crazy at times but in this book I actually got to see a softer side of Alex that I really liked, and I can say she is still the same crazy Alex that us fans love but she is also maturing and growing and I love the new Alex!<br><br><b>Aiden</b> You all probaly already heard me say this but......I AM NOW #TEAMAIDEN !!!<br>I was originally Team Seth because he was hotter and funny than the boring Aiden but Aiden has stepped up his GAME this time around! I LOVE HIM! I WANT TO MARRY HIM! HAVE SENTINAL BABIES WITH HIM!....Anyways, Aiden finally has a chance to show us the real him and I am LOVING ALL OF IT! He is soooooo sweet, loving and caring when it comes to Alex, you can't help but love him! All my #TeamSeth girls look out because Aiden is going to steal your heart!<br><br><br><b>Seth</b> Oh, Seth........Hmmmmmmmm......I suggest you guys should read the book when it comes out to see why I have no words for him. I still love you Seth, but you need to get it together!!!!! I will have more to say about him Nov 6th so look out :)<br><br><br><b>Leon</b> I know you guys are wondering why I am mentioning Leon in my review because he is a 'nobody' but I think everyone will notice his role in book three and come to LOVE HIM!<br><br><b>Minister Telly</b> I HATE YOU AND WISH YOU WOULD DIE!!!<br><br><b>Lucian</b> I just DON'T LIKE YOU!!!<br><br><b>Romance:</b> LOTS OF IT!!!! I loved this book for the steamy parts that popped in and out of this book, all of them will leave you with an AWWWWWWW feeling :) &lt;3<br><br><br><b>Action:</b> OMGGGGG!!! There is so much action in this book you will not be able to put it down. So many surprises that you can't even guess what is going to happen next and that is my kind of book!<br><br><b>Plot</b> Was so AWESOME! You guys are not going to believe which of the Gods make an appearance in this book an oh, the Furies are back!<br><br><br><b>Overall:</b> This book was EPIC!!!! And I can't wait to discuss Deity with you all! I will be adding more to my review once it comes out because I am DYING to get it all out!!<br><br><br>Rating: GR for GOOD READ!!!!<br><br><br>Until next time!<br><br>Thanks for listening!<br><br>-Alice &lt;3<br><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16096515058120022899"><b>WELL...</b><br/><br/>There were things that <i>sucked</i> daimon butt,<br/>there were things that <i>kicked</i> daimon butt.<br/>Everything I was dreading would happen,<br/>happened but the romance aside,<br/>Deity was awesome.<br/>There's the same humor, <br/>action, && sexiness in Deity<br/>that we're accustomed to in all Jenn's books<br/>Always entertaining && hard to put down.<br/>Even when things are happening<br/>that just rip you apart.<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[<br/><br/>Alex chose Aiden. I knew it would happen. (so I made this gif)<br/><a href='http://s1129.photobucket.com/albums/m504/StOrMyAnDjJ/?action=view&current=Damongif.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365539ra/717659.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> (I'm not sure if Alex will ever feel THAT way with hi</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16096515058120022899" style="display:none"><b>WELL...</b><br><br>There were things that <i>sucked</i> daimon butt,<br>there were things that <i>kicked</i> daimon butt.<br>Everything I was dreading would happen,<br>happened but the romance aside,<br>Deity was awesome.<br>There's the same humor, <br>action, &amp;&amp; sexiness in Deity<br>that we're accustomed to in all Jenn's books<br>Always entertaining &amp;&amp; hard to put down.<br>Even when things are happening<br>that just rip you apart.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Alex chose Aiden. I knew it would happen. (so I made this gif)<br><a href="http://s1129.photobucket.com/albums/m504/StOrMyAnDjJ/?action=view&amp;current=Damongif.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380365539ra/717659.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> (I'm not sure if Alex will ever feel THAT way with him but I hope she does forget how good he can be) <br>We all knew it would happen. I can't say I was shocked. I expected it to happen just like it happened. Something drastic had to happen to Alex (her death) for him to break free of the rules and admit his feelings and finally be with her. Totally predicted that. I can't say that I hate him. SHOCKER! I found respect for him in Deity. He stopped with the pushing and pulling and all the games and just manned up. That's all I was waiting for. His love for Alex is obvious and genuine. I always thought he was boring but seeing how he lightened up with Alex, I actually liked that, that he could be funny. I know the perfect song for them. Treacherous - Taylor Swift. So, I'm not mad that she's with him, I'm just disappointed in the path Seth's character has taken. His character always lightened up situations and that's what I loved about him. He was...<br><a href="http://s1129.photobucket.com/albums/m504/StOrMyAnDjJ/?action=view&amp;current=Untitled-2.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379770099i/284983.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br>He was the fun in all the drama that was Alex's life and now the positions are reversed and he's the drama. WHAT THE HELL!? Turns out he had nefarious plans, lies, and betrayal burning up his whole relationship with Alex. I actually kind of like the evil bad boy thing as long as his feelings are genuine when it comes to the girl but with Seth, it's kind of hard to tell. He's so cocky and egotistical with all this extra energy flowing through him and changing him. He takes everything someone says and does as a challenge. This wasn't the Seth we were introduced to and I feel betrayed every bit as much as Alex does. I had hope just like she did. I mean, he has to care for her, that all couldn't have been faked. Could it? I saw his care for her behind his actions. I know that's just gotta be the Apollyon power and his pain of what he went through in life and probably the fact that he isn't a star of Alex's affections, not him - the real him. Gods, I have so much hope for him still. I hope he doesn't trash that. I hope he doesn't push Alex to do awful things. I hope he pulls through, out of the insanity. I hope he doesn't die. I hope he can at least be a friend to Alex in the end. I just wish that Alex would figure out how to take power from him already. She's done it before when she blew up that rock. She knows she can do it and Artemis mentioned it. I just want to give her a big DUH. She should have figured that out a long time ago and maybe prevented things from happening. She never even tried to really use her powers though. Ugh. So frustrating. <br><br>Anyway, I like the whole dying and going to the Underworld part. It was closure with Caleb. She needed that. I was hoping she would get to see her mom. Where the heck is her dad though? He up and disappeared without a trace. Just wondering when we'll get to meet him. The clerk in the store cracked me up, along with Apollo. He likes to freak them out by poofing in and out with his godly eyes. He's so awesome. Deacon and Luke, so sweet! LOL As always there are plenty sarcastic and funny remarks to keep you rolling. <br><br>Oh goodness, I cant even think anymore. I'm just so drained from all this... Missing my Sethy Bear from Pure... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_242375197" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/242375197" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/242375197?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ♥Rachel♥ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1894085-alexa">Alexa</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer242375197" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15419771057612821398">Wow! I think The Covenant series just keeps getting better and better! Deity is my favorite so far!<br/><br/>Alex is back home and training but repercussions from the events at the council are not going away. With the attack by the Daemons, the Furies showing up, and all the death and destruction that followed, their world is in upheaval. Plus, Alex is worried it will come out that she was responsible for the death of a Pure, and that Aiden covered it up. It won’t matter that is was in self-defense. Plus,</span>
  <span id="freeText15419771057612821398" style="display:none">Wow! I think The Covenant series just keeps getting better and better! Deity is my favorite so far!<br /><br />Alex is back home and training but repercussions from the events at the council are not going away. With the attack by the Daemons, the Furies showing up, and all the death and destruction that followed, their world is in upheaval. Plus, Alex is worried it will come out that she was responsible for the death of a Pure, and that Aiden covered it up. It won’t matter that is was in self-defense. Plus, Prime Minister Telly is hot on Alex’s tail, paying a special visit just to see her. Alex has also been spending a lot of time with Seth but she can’t shake the idea that theirs is a physical attraction only, and is she really willing to settle on that? Also, Alex is counting down the days to her Awakening. She’s afraid of what she might become and how much of herself she’ll lose once she Awakens. <br /><br />I have to say in Pure, I was growing tired of Alex’s rash and reckless actions. She was playing right into the hands of the very ones that wanted to enslave her. This was really starting to annoy me. I’m happy to report that in Deity, we see some major character growth and she seemed to smarten up and mature considerably. I’m so pleased with the turn of events! Alex is also starting to question the ways of her society, and no longer just taking things as she’s told. <br /><br />I don’t think I’ve ever loved Aiden more than in this book! Oh my heart!! ♥♥♥ He’s by Alex’s side and is her fierce protector, unwavering throughout! I am SO Team Aiden!!! Seth is sexy, for sure, but his motives are always under suspicion, in my opinion; even more so as we have some revelations. Okay, I have to give you a steamy quote but I won’t tell you the parties involved, so it’s not spoilery:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>My fingers sifted through his hair as I held him to me. His kisses were doing crazy, strange, and wonderful things to me. I whispered his name over and over again like some kind of mad prayer. Then I was moving against him, being guided by some primal instinct that told me what to do.*</i>
</b><br /><br />In Pure I was left with so many questions, I found it a bit frustrating. But in Deity we have answers!! I was shocked by one in particular. We finally get to find out why they don’t want Pures and Half-Bloods together. Deity reveals many things, and I have a much clearer picture now. However, the ending killed me!! Oh no you didn’t Jennifer!! I think some quality time on the naughty rug might be in order!<br /><br />Jennifer L. Armentrout has a talent for sucking you into a story so you can’t put it down, it’s just impossible! The Covenant Series is highly addictive! I can’t wait until Apollyon! April can’t come soon enough. <br /><br />You can find this review and more at <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den </a>. <br /><br />Thank you to Spencer Hill Press for allowing me to read this! <br /><br />*Quote taken from an uncorrected proof and my change in the final copy. <br /><br /><br /><b>Below you will see my original thoughts I had after reading this. :)</b><br /><br /><b>OH NO YOU DIDN'T, JENNIFER!!!</b> You did <b>NOT</b> just end it there!!! I think you need a time-out on the naughty rug!!<br /><br />With that said, DEITY is my favorite of the Covenant series! Oh Aiden!!♥♥♥ <br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9897164.Apollyon__Covenant___4_" title="Apollyon (Covenant, #4) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Apollyon</a> can't come soon enough.<br /><br />Proper review to come closer to the release date. <br /><br />A huge thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1894085-alexa" rel="nofollow noopener">Alexa</a> for lending me her precious copy!! I got to read this before Spencer Hill sent out their copy to me thanks to her. </span>
  <a data-text-id="15419771057612821398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4591480757941982176"><pre>
  <b>“Sometimes you have to know when to let hope go.”</b>
</pre><br/>ASDFGHJKL this has got to be one of the <i>
  <b>worst</b>
</i> cliffhangers ever.😰😓<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602443841ra/30224359.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>The <b>betrayal</b>.....The <b>pain</b>.....The <b>fear</b>.....The <b>LOVE</b>🥺<br/><b>IT'S ALL TOO MUCH😭</b><br/><br/>Seriously though, each book in the series just keeps getting better and better.💖 I love these guys so much, although some <i>people</i> have made some.......<i>questionable</i> choices and it's so sad.😣<br/><br/><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS BELOW FROM PREVIOUS BOOKS!!!🛑</u>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>“That simple act stole my breath, my heart. But even as he pulle</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText4591480757941982176" style="display:none"><pre>
  <b>“Sometimes you have to know when to let hope go.”</b>
</pre><br>ASDFGHJKL this has got to be one of the <i>
  <b>worst</b>
</i> cliffhangers ever.😰😓<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602443841ra/30224359.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The <b>betrayal</b>.....The <b>pain</b>.....The <b>fear</b>.....The <b>LOVE</b>🥺<br><b>IT'S ALL TOO MUCH😭</b><br><br>Seriously though, each book in the series just keeps getting better and better.💖 I love these guys so much, although some <i>people</i> have made some.......<i>questionable</i> choices and it's so sad.😣<br><br><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS BELOW FROM PREVIOUS BOOKS!!!🛑</u>
</b><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“That simple act stole my breath, my heart. But even as he pulled away, I realized that he couldn't steal something he already had.”</blockquote>
</b><br><b>Omg how sweet is that?!?!🥺😭😍</b> Alex has changed so much from the first book, but the one thing that <b>
  <i>never</i>
</b> changed was her love for Aiden. Aghhhh I'm about to start crying now.🥺 Their love for each other makes my heart swell with emotion. She's had to deal with so much death (<i>like Caleb's</i>) and guilt, but now she's learned from most of her mistakes and aghhh just the growth.....<b>I love it</b>.💞<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I can’t keep pretending that I don’t want this – that I don’t want you. I can’t. Not after what happened to you. It thought… I thought I’d lost you, Alex, forever. And I would’ve lost everything. You <i>are</i> my everything.”</blockquote>
</b><br>AHHH AIDEN!!!! <b>I LOVE AIDEN SO MUCH😍😍😍</b> He's the sweetest guy ever and JLA always manages to do it perfectly.🥺 Aiden loves Alex and <i>
  <b>always</b>
</i> keeps the promises he makes for her <i>(unlike <b>some</b> people)</i>. Omg and every time Aiden calls Alex <b>
  <i>"Agapi mou"</i>
</b>......my heart just melts.🤧🥰 <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602445683ra/30224423.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Haha but the fights between <b>Seth</b> and <b>Aiden</b> over Alex were priceless.😆🤣 At one point even <b>Leon</b> and <b>Seth</b> had a go at it. It was way too funny xD. <br><b>
  <blockquote>He sneered. “You want to fight me now, in your<br>true form?”<br>“I will fight you in any form, you little punk-ass brat.”<br>Seth laughed. “You can’t kill me.”<br>“But I can beat the living snot out of you.”</blockquote>
</b><br>I love Leon.😆 He's such an awesome guy. And to Alex, he's know as <b>"The King of Impeccable Timing"</b>, which I definitely agree with xD. He has the <b>
  <i>worst timing</i>
</b> with certain moments, but you could also say that those appearances prevent some......decisions.😂<br><br>Oh that reminds me. Speaking of people with bad decisions.....<b>Seth</b>😞. I was never a <b>Team Seth</b> to begin with, but some of the things he did weren't really good. HE CAN'T SEE THAT <b>STUPID LUCIEN</b> IS <b>
  <i>USING</i>
</b> HIM!!!😫😤 And now....well things aren't really looking that good.😓 But I was happy with what happened to <b>Telly</b>—he had that coming and also, I can't believe that his name means "Best".😶 The only thing he's "best" at is pissing me off.😤<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602461514ra/30225055.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were some others that appeared much more, too. Like <b>Deacon</b>, whom I also just adore.😍 His parts were hilarious xD. <br><blockquote>
  <b>“Yeah, I'm great. Nothing like witnessing a death match between gods when I'm trying to get some Cheetos.</b>
</blockquote><br>^Poor Deacon.....he just wanted to eat his Cheetos.😢<br><br>The appearances of some of the Greek Gods was probably my fav part (that and a <i>certain</i> 2 people finally being together.🥰🥺). Apollo of course, is the funniest and coolest God of all of them hehe. I can't wait to see more of his scenes—Oh and his <b>poofing.</b>😆<br><br>Sadly, there won't be many fun times with these guys because.......<br><br><b>🔥𝐖𝐚𝐫 𝐢𝐬 𝐜𝐨𝐦𝐢𝐧𝐠🔥</b></span>

<div id="review_230686233" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/230686233" />
    <a title="Marie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6594537-marie"><img alt="Marie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535710504p2/6594537.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/230686233?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marie" href="/user/show/6594537-marie">Marie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=good">good</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=gods-and-godesses">gods-and-godesses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer230686233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5162940170273197400">Ok so before reading this I hoped Alex would wake-up and choose to be with Seth. <br/><br/>Now I'm probably insane but that hasn't changed what so ever. <br/><br/>Now before all you Aiden fans attack me, I know Seth is a bit screwed up right now and has become an enraged murderer, a little toy for Lucian to take over the world with. <br/><br/>BUT IS THAT REALLY HIM? No. He's got a fucked up past and only wants to be loved. Lucian's manipulating him and it makes me sick. I'm not giving up on him when he needs Alex and everyon</span>
  <span id="freeText5162940170273197400" style="display:none">Ok so before reading this I hoped Alex would wake-up and choose to be with Seth. <br /><br />Now I'm probably insane but that hasn't changed what so ever. <br /><br />Now before all you Aiden fans attack me, I know Seth is a bit screwed up right now and has become an enraged murderer, a little toy for Lucian to take over the world with. <br /><br />BUT IS THAT REALLY HIM? No. He's got a fucked up past and only wants to be loved. Lucian's manipulating him and it makes me sick. I'm not giving up on him when he needs Alex and everyone now more than ever. <br />I believe he can be saved. So many have given up on him already it makes me so sad. <br />I want Alex to save him and fall for him in the process. :)<br /><br />Now the book. It is not my favourite book of the series by far. I mean Seth was finally gaining some ground on the Seth and Alex romance when she turns him into a psycho. No. But I do like where the stories leading and the fact that the true goss have finally made an appearance.<br />This book starts right where Pure left off and finished with Alex's awakening. And my gods the cliffhanger at the end will leave you shaking and craving for the next book like a Daimon shaking and craving for their next fix of aether. <br /><br />If your Aiden fans stop reading now.<br />However for all you Seth fans these are Seth and Alex's best scenes in this book.<br /><br /> 1. <b> <br />“Seth’s body tensed. “Good gods…”<br />And then I felt it—akasha—shifting through the cords, leaving me and entering Seth. It was kind of like a daimon tag, but not painful. No… this was nice, heady. I stopped struggling, letting the glorious tug and pull lift me away. I didn’t think about anything. There were no concerns or fears. The pain in my hand melted away, leaving only a dull ache that was spreading elsewhere. There was just this… and Seth. My eyes drifted shut and a sigh leaked out. Why had I been so afraid of this?<br />There was a flash of light that I could still see even though my eyes were closed. Seth dropped my hand and it fell limply to my side. The bed dipped beside my head from where he placed his hands. I felt his breath on my cheek, and it felt like warm, salty air rolling off the ocean.<br />“Alex?”<br />“Hmm…?”<br />“You okay?” He placed his lips to my cheek.<br />I smiled.<br />Seth chuckled, and then his mouth was making its way to mine, and I opened for him. The edges of his hair tickled my cheeks as the kiss deepened. His fingers drifted down the front of my blouse and then they were sliding over the bare skin of my stomach. I wrapped my leg around his, and we were moving together on the bed. His lips were dancing all over my flushed skin as his hands slid down, fingers finding the button on my jeans.<br />A second later, there was a knock on my door and a booming voice. “Alexandria?”<br />Seth stilled above me, panting. “You have got to be freaking kidding me.”<br />Leon knocked again. “Alexandria, I know you’re in there.”<br />Dazed, I blinked several times. The room slowly came back into focus, as did Seth’s disgruntled expression. I almost laughed, except I felt… off.”<br /><br /></b> 2. <b> <br />“I flushed as I put my hands on his chest, stopping him from overcoming that last inch or two that separated us. “People “change,” I said lamely.<br />“Some people do.” He placed his arm beside my head, supporting himself.<br />The cord was really starting to go crazy, demanding that I pay attention to it. My toes curled. “Did you come here to talk about the rules I’ve broken or what?”<br />“No. I actually had a reason for coming.”<br />“And that is?” I shifted uncomfortably, trying to ignore the way my skin, especially the palms of my hands, started to tingle. Thank the gods he had a shirt on.<br />“Give me a second.”<br />I frowned. “Why do—”<br />Seth dipped his head, brushing his lips over mine, and being caught between wanting to clamp my mouth shut and wanting to open for him was a frustrating feeling. I ached to be near him as equally as I did to be away from him.<br />“That’s… that’s why you came here?” I asked when he lifted his head.<br />“It wasn’t the main reason.”<br />“Then why are you—” His mouth cut my words off, and the kiss deepened, stealing my protests. The cord tightened as his hand slipped down my arm, over my stomach and under the hem of my shirt.<br />He smiled against my lips.<br /><br /></b> 3. <b><br />“But why do you have to go?”<br />“I don’t know, Alex. Can we talk about this later?” He looked down at me, eyes glowing. “There are other things I want to do.”<br />The cord buzzed its approval. “But—”<br />Seth kissed me again and the hand against my stomach pressed down. I let go of his wrist, intending on pushing him off, but then I was gripping his shirt. The air around us seemed to crackle. There was something building inside me, a warning that the damn bond was up to no good.<br />I felt the cord rushing to the surface before I actually opened my eyes. Amber and blue lights cast strange shadows across the wall of my bedroom. I was transfixed by them for a moment. It was so bizarre that we were responsible for them. That they even came from within us.”<br /><br />“It freaked me out a little.<br />But Seth’s free hand was everywhere, skimming down my arm, over my leg, and our cords were spiraling together, connecting us. My fingers clenched his shirt and I was pulling him down.<br /><br /></b> 4. <b><br />“He dropped his shoes and swept his arms around me. “You drive me crazy.”<br />“I know.” I smiled. “The feeling is mutual.”<br />He laughed and then brushed his lips over my forehead. “Come on.” He started pulling me back to the bed.<br />I stalled a little. Not hurting his feelings did not equal me ending up with a mark on the back of my neck.<br />Seth dropped down, tugging me forward. “To sleep, Alex. Nothing more… unless…” His gaze dropped to my tank top. “You know, you should wear that more often. It leaves very little to the imagination, which is something I like.”<br />Flushing to the roots of my hair, I quickly climbed over him and pulled the covers up to my chin. Seth laughed as he lay down. He threw an arm around my waist, snuggling close. His breathing was steady. Nothing like mine, which seemed to be racing my heartbeat. And he was smiling easily, as if we hadn’t just argued.<br />“You’re such a perv,” I said for the hundredth time.<br />“You’ve called me worse.”<br />And I had a feeling I probably would in the future, too.”<br /><br /></b> And finally-5. <b> <br /><br />“The First—my whole purpose for existing. Mine. My other half. He was here, waiting. Already inside me, seeing what I was seeing, whispering to me, promising me that he was coming. Seth. Mine.”<br /><br /><br /></b> All 5 are excerpts from: Armentrout, Jennifer L. “Deity (Covenant).” Spencer Hill Press.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5162940170273197400" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1056864927" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1056864927?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1056864927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer188889705505544174"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/stars_zpsb430dd63.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411089539i/11192653.jpg' alt=' photo stars_zpsb430dd63.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Deity is book three in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I have loved every book so far in this series but something happened to me about half way through this third book. That feeling hit, that obsessed feeling when you can’t think of anything else but what is going on in the book. That feeling when you just want to close yourself off in a room and read non-stop. This was by far my favorite of the series so far. So much was revealed in this book. Our characters are all growing and</span>
  <span id="freeText188889705505544174" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/stars_zpsb430dd63.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411089539i/11192653.jpg" alt=" photo stars_zpsb430dd63.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Deity is book three in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. I have loved every book so far in this series but something happened to me about half way through this third book. That feeling hit, that obsessed feeling when you can’t think of anything else but what is going on in the book. That feeling when you just want to close yourself off in a room and read non-stop. This was by far my favorite of the series so far. So much was revealed in this book. Our characters are all growing and changing as well. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/dagger_zps0d3d2a45.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411089539i/11192654.jpg" alt=" photo dagger_zps0d3d2a45.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Alex, oh Alex. She has been manipulated, lied to, and deceived. Continued attempts have been made on her life. She is scared to death of the awakening. But she is loyal to a fault.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n0tyh6ENJS1rg028zo1_500_zpsa44ea553.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411089539i/11192655._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n0tyh6ENJS1rg028zo1_500_zpsa44ea553.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>So much is revealed in this book. Some concerns I have had from the start have proved true. I was pleasantly surprised by one particular ally. And we got a new character that is on Alex’s side. Something I did not expect at all. Along with this new character Alex’s lineage is also revealed.<br><br>So much happened in this book and I am trying hard not to give anything away. We finally learn how Apollyons are conceived. And we learn the true evil plans in place for using the power of Alex and Seth once they are connected. We get to know Deacon (Aiden’s brother) better in this book and I want to say that I love him. Actually, it seems that there are more Team Alex members than she thought. Alex thought she was alone, abandoned by everyone. But she truly is not. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/chain_zpsdc5a774f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411089539i/11192656.jpg" alt=" photo chain_zpsdc5a774f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Now let’s talk about Aiden. I was so frustrated with him in the previous books. He always held Alex’s heart, even though she thought he didn’t want it. But in this book he finally reveals his true self to her. And I melted into a puddle on the floor. It was that wonderful. <br><br><b>
  <i>“You’ll have a piece of my heart--all of it, really. Forever.”</i>
</b><br><br>This book had me going from my heart beating out of my chest in fear to my heart melting with some of the sweetest moments. Then there was the “Oh My Gosh, that did NOT just happen!” <br><br>I think now we are beginning to wonder what is strongest, the power of true love, or the power of a supernatural connection. It is a true test of good vs. evil. And talk about a cliff hanger. We are left barely hanging on by our fingernails. It’s a good thing I am binge reading this series and will be immediately going on to the next book. Otherwise, I don’t know how I would have been able to stand it. <br><br>Looking back over this review, I don’t really think I said much of anything. Just know that this book was fantastic. My favorite so far. And that I can’t wait to continue on. And that if you haven’t started this series yet, DO…SO…RIGHT…NOW!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>“Agapi mou, zoi mou”<br>“My love, my life.”</i>
</b> <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125365.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098482.jpg" alt=" photo ja_zps16dd050b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1056864927">

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer361019454" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2683983337191856923"><b>OMG!!!!!! THAT ENDING!!!! THAT ENDING!!!! SPEECHLESS!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><i>5 AMAZING STARS!!!!</i><br/><br/>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382810ra/740870.gif' alt=' photo amazing_zps8f726130.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <b>Wow!! This book was unbelievable!! So shocking!!!! That ending blew my mind!!! </b>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382810ra/740871.gif' alt=' photo mindblown_zps9139d137.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm so glad this series has finally found its own path and can now step out of Vampire Academy's shadow. Deity is fast-paced and full of plot twists that will blow your mind. I can honestly say this is the best book in the series so far. I absolutely loved it!!! <br/><br/>I love Alex!!! She is a strong determined woman who will do </span>
  <span id="freeText2683983337191856923" style="display:none"><b>OMG!!!!!! THAT ENDING!!!! THAT ENDING!!!! SPEECHLESS!!!!!!</b><br><br><i>5 AMAZING STARS!!!!</i><br><br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382810ra/740870.gif" alt=" photo amazing_zps8f726130.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
  <b>Wow!! This book was unbelievable!! So shocking!!!! That ending blew my mind!!! </b>
  <br>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382810ra/740871.gif" alt=" photo mindblown_zps9139d137.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so glad this series has finally found its own path and can now step out of Vampire Academy's shadow. Deity is fast-paced and full of plot twists that will blow your mind. I can honestly say this is the best book in the series so far. I absolutely loved it!!! <br><br>I love Alex!!! She is a strong determined woman who will do anything to keep the people close to her safe even if it means giving up her own life for the cause. I’m really starting to see the character growth in Alex. Instead of running off and doing something extremely stupid, she thinks before she acts. Well let me rephrase that, she thinks before she acts some of the time. Alex still needs to work on that, but she is way better in this book than the previous books. I still think she is very naïve. She tries to see the good in everyone when maybe there isn’t any good left. I can relate to her in that aspect because I have the same problem. <br><br>I adore Aiden!! He might act like a jealous asshole at times but I still love him. I was so happy when he finally told Alex the truth about how he feels for her, but I will say it was really fun to watch him get jealous of how much time Seth was spending with Alex. I can’t wait to see where their relationship is going to go even if it is forbidden. <br><br><b>All I can say about Seth is he showed his true colors in this book. I was so shocked!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380382810ra/740872.gif" alt=" photo noooo_zps1f5b997f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I actually liked Seth and thought he genuinely cared for Alex, but I was so wrong on all ends. I realized that Seth has only been looking out for himself. All he wants is <i>POWER </i>and he doesn’t care who gets hurt in the process. Part of me hopes Alex can save him in some kind of way but I feel like it’s going to end badly for him.<br><br>Overall, I loved this book and the series!!! I can’t wait to see what going to happen in the next!! Definitely a must read!!!!
</span>

<div id="review_220382108" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220382108" />
    <a title="~Tina~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2594672-tina"><img alt="~Tina~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411474324p2/2594672.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220382108?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Tina~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Tina~" href="/user/show/2594672-tina">~Tina~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=own-copy">own-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=jennifer-rocks">jennifer-rocks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2594672-tina?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220382108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1225664753659122707">Originally I was going to go all screaming-fan-girl on ya'll, but I decided that I wanted the readers to experience this book the way I did, so while there is some spoilers, I kept this as spoil-free as much as possible.<br/><br/><b>Undeniably Epic!</b><br/><br/>Jennifer L. Armentrout third installment in the <i>Covenant</i> series is nothing short of brilliance. It surpassed all of my wildest expectations and then some. This series is an unstoppable force, bringing something fresh and powerful to the world of mythology as well </span>
  <span id="freeText1225664753659122707" style="display:none">Originally I was going to go all screaming-fan-girl on ya'll, but I decided that I wanted the readers to experience this book the way I did, so while there is some spoilers, I kept this as spoil-free as much as possible.<br><br><b>Undeniably Epic!</b><br><br>Jennifer L. Armentrout third installment in the <i>Covenant</i> series is nothing short of brilliance. It surpassed all of my wildest expectations and then some. This series is an unstoppable force, bringing something fresh and powerful to the world of mythology as well as inspiring endless emotions from pure joy to pure rage to action punched- spine tingling-on the verge of being thrown from my seat- excitement.<br> <br>Someone once asked me between the Lux series and this one, which was my favorite book.<br>Picking a favorite JLA book is like asking me which of my children I love more. It's impossible to choose. <br>I love them all. Hard and equally.<br>But I still have to ask, how the hell does she do it?!? I swear there is nothing, I repeat, nothing like being inside a JLA novel. My insides were a rush of energy and a puddle of goo. Alex may have a cord pulsing in her stomach but mine had a swarm of butterflies doing the hula dance. I love/adore/worship the way this women can write. I even smiled to myself when the words <i>obsidian</i> and <i>onyx</i> would play into a sentence. Reminding me that aliens or mythology or even adult contemporary, this women doesn't hold back. She gives us her heart and soul and it shines through every single one of her characters. <br><br><b>Deity</b> was a surge of pure adrenaline. There are so many epic twist in this book and so many moments that I have a hard time believing any of this was real. Like a freaken dream. I was floored in the best way possible.<br>There is just to many things that happened plot-wise to even try to explain. Compared to Pure, this book steps up in a gigantic way. No skimming room for this one folks, your gonna want to hang on ever word and hold on to your seats cause this is one helluva explosive ride. Things just got freaken serious. Fans are gonna eat this alive. <br><br>I don't even know where to start with these characters, they were all simply outstanding. <br>Deacon, Luke, Leon and even Lenard are just a few that had effected the story line in a way that left me in awe. Especially Leon. I have to say that he was my favorite twist. I always liked him just fine, but now I simply adore him. I can't wait to see more of him in the next coming books. <br>~I am so so proud of Alex. I new that she was destined for greatness, but I didn't think she would be this incredible. This girl has grown into a fierce force. Her compassion is astounding. Her bravery and strength admirable and her humor and easy personality makes her simply irresistible. The way she didn't want to give up on Seth almost killed me since apart of me doesn't think he deserves it, but in true Alex fashion she even has me believing in hope. <br>Such a fantastic character.<br>~Aiden totally owned this book. I wasn't to pleased with him in the last book, but yeah, he totally made up for it.<br>I love love loved seeing this sweet and playful and affectionate side to him besides the already established protectiveness and loyal qualities he possesses. There were so many treasured moments that made my heart stop and took my breath away. My heart hurt I was so happy. I'm also glad we finally know what <i>agapi mou, zoi mou</i> means now. I melted I tell ya. Reading those Alex and Aiden scenes reminded me of what young first love was all about. The dip in your belly every time he comes into a room. The perma-smile that's plastered on your face when you even think his name. These two makes me believe in love and that anything and everything is possible.<br>~Now for Seth. ~sigh~ I am truly conflicted. My first reaction after reading this was that I indeed hate him. I've always been Team Aiden all the way, but Seth managed to wiggle some love in the last book, but now? Not so much. He did things that hurt to even read, I'm not even sure he can be redeemed in my eyes. His greed for ultimate power clouded everything good and real about him and I just don't know what to believe anymore. I am awfully curious what JLA has in store for his character. I'm nervous and scared as hell.<br>~It was also so great to see one of my favorite characters, even if it was just a little scene. It brought peace to my heart just as much as it did for Alex.<br><br>I feel like I can go on and on praising this wonderful gem, but the truth is no matter what I say it will never bring this book justice. Fan of this incredible women and this incredible series are going to love this. The writing it pulse pounding pitch perfect and insanely entertaining. The story line took us on a whole new level of oh.my.gods and these characters will make you heart explode.<br><br>Pure Awesomesauce!<br><br> NEED.APOLLYON.NOW!!!!<br><br>HUGE thanks to SpencerHill Press for sending me an arc in exchange for a honest review. I'm hugging you right now!<br><br><br>:My first reaction after reading this book:<br><br>OMG! That ending?!?!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/friends%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360805ra/711705.gif" alt="friends gifs Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yup, this pretty much describes what I'm feeling right about now.<br><br>Best.JLA.Book.Evah!!!!!<br></span>

<div id="review_311778783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/311778783" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/311778783?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=own-a-dtb">own-a-dtb</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=just-another-book-crush">just-another-book-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=creepy-love-triangle">creepy-love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=my-flat-army">my-flat-army</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=arc-2012">arc-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=random-house">random-house</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer311778783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1716359822338118390">From now on, the year 2012 shall be known as The Year of Cliffhangers and Jennifer L. Armentrout as the person responsible. Two in a row is more than I can take. Why not just hand me a rope to hang myself with instead? Where are the Furies when you need them?<br/><br/>This will be a moderately short review because there really isn't much to write about. With Pure and Deity (and Opal), Armentrout restored my faith in her and and turned me into an addict. I have now grudgingly joined hordes of fans who eage</span>
  <span id="freeText1716359822338118390" style="display:none">From now on, the year 2012 shall be known as The Year of Cliffhangers and Jennifer L. Armentrout as the person responsible. Two in a row is more than I can take. Why not just hand me a rope to hang myself with instead? Where are the Furies when you need them?<br><br>This will be a moderately short review because there really isn't much to write about. With Pure and Deity (and Opal), Armentrout restored my faith in her and and turned me into an addict. I have now grudgingly joined hordes of fans who eagerly await her every release. <br><br>It’s not all roses and rainbows, though. I think what's stopping this series from truly becoming one of my favorites is that, thanks to the Half-Blood debacle, I can't stop comparing it to Vampire Academy. Even though Alex is now a heroine in her own right, a part of me still sees her as a pale copy of Rose Hathaway. The same goes for Aiden – as amazing as he is (and trust me, he is one amazing guy), I can't help but compare him to Dimitri on occasion, and of course he loses every time. That is the consequence of Armentrout's initial plagiarism. Although she found a different path for her characters (and hopefully for herself), all those connections my mind made at the beginning simply refuse to go away. <br><br>Although reluctantly, I feel that I must also mention a series of editing issues I’ve come across in Deity. Awkward, clumsy sentences and incorrect word order are just some of the things a more careful reader will surely notice. This could have easily been avoided which is why it upset me so much. <br><br>But I didn’t set out to write a negative review. Deity set a new course for this series, an expected one perhaps, but a new and satisfying direction nonetheless. Aside from the horrendous cliffhanger, I have no objections whatsoever. With Deity, Armentrout gave me exactly what I’ve learned to expect from her. As for the said cliffhanger, I’ve been told that Elixir, a novella from Aiden’s point of view, really takes the edge off and I’m looking forward to it. <br><br>Without revealing too much, I'll try to ease the minds of those who are like me: the (in)famous love triangle finally gets resolved in this book, or at least Alex sees things for what they really are. If you’re anything like me, you were severely annoyed by the Aiden-Alex-Seth mess in the second book, but rest assured, it does get better. <br><br><b>
  <i>That simple act stole my breath, my heart. But even as he pulled away, I realized that he couldn't steal something he already had.</i>
</b><br><br>At this point, I'd say I'm enjoying this series despite myself. It is extremely addictive and fun, but at the same time, I can't forget how it started. Perhaps with Apollyon, Armentrout will break those last stubborn connections and make me look at this series differently. Either way, I'm looking forward to it. <br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1716359822338118390" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1803727183" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1803727183" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1803727183?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-and-action">love-and-action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=something-new">something-new</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=fantasy-paranormal">fantasy-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=funny-as-hell">funny-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1803727183" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1322071199495954174">This  is my favorite book so far, I just loved it top to bottom and I've read it with amazing speed, because its THAT addictive. I loved every second of it and consider it the best in action and twist of events. <br/><br/>"Deity" begins in a low pace, but after that, the action builds up and makes you gasp every step of the way. Alex is months away from Awakening and this means she has to be ready for the danger that may come. Her connection with Seth is stronger than ever and her confusion is getting the</span>
  <span id="freeText1322071199495954174" style="display:none">This  is my favorite book so far, I just loved it top to bottom and I've read it with amazing speed, because its THAT addictive. I loved every second of it and consider it the best in action and twist of events. <br><br>"Deity" begins in a low pace, but after that, the action builds up and makes you gasp every step of the way. Alex is months away from Awakening and this means she has to be ready for the danger that may come. Her connection with Seth is stronger than ever and her confusion is getting the best of her. She began to care about him but in the same time she doesn't trust him, not knowing exactly what his true intentions are. She finds out certain things about him, but as you know Alex, she believes Seth can be saved. To put it worst, somebody is trying to kill her and she will have to be heavily guarded in order to stay safe. All the book is centered on the days until her Awakening and how will she act and feel upon it. <br><br>Alex is a different character now, letting aside her temper and personality that were untouched, but she is more focused, more mature and more willing to take chances for the things she loves. I have to admit, I like her a lot, considering her very atypical and extremely funny. She knows how to be vulnerable, but also very feisty and straightforward. She is very afraid of becoming an Apollyon and will do anything necessary to use her powers in a good manner.<br><br>Aiden!! Aiden!! Aiden!!! Wow, he definitely has a place in my Book Boyfriends Top.. I loved him in this book and I wanted to tell him "IT WAS ABOUT TIME" !!! Aiden personality and intentions shifted dramatically in "Deity" after a certain chain of events. You will see for yourself and consider this happenings positive for our couple. His tender and nurture side will be mostly present, his wall completely down and willing to love Alex against all rules. He will fight for her and prove to us what we already knew from the beginning, that he's a terrific hero. <br><br>With Seth I'm in the "No comment" area because there is not much to say about..I don't like him and I hope Alex will show him the right path. I have faith that she will succeed, because the situation in which they are right now really sucks:)<br><br>The book was amazing and I liked the construction of it tremendously. It had every ingredient necessary to keep you alert 100%. The characters evolved in a normal pace, some predictable, some not, but they were a whole and everyone had with purpose. The romantic scenes were incredibly written, Jennifer giving the right amount of love and steaminess for them not to be very descriptive, but for you to understand exactly the message and connect with it immediately. It was the perfect mixture and this one had more OMG moments and scenes where you were left dizzy and wanting for more. Here you will find all the answers you'll be waiting for and your suspicions will maybe become reality. <br><br>Next is "Apollyon".. Only 2 more books to go:( <br><br>5 stars!<br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1322071199495954174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer256613870" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18185201526710380699">OHHHHHHH MYYYYYYYYYY GOOOOOOOOOOOOOOD! <br/><br/>WOW, JLA you never cease to amaze me with your awesomeness. I am so completely drained from this book. I am sick to my stomach and seriously am scared shitless for what's to come in Apollyon. But holy hell....that was freakin badass!<br/><br/><br/>I am too tired and exhausted to write this review since my brain has been shut off. So I will stop here and leave you with...<br/><br/><br/>TEAM AIDEX ALWAYS!!!!! I don't care, something will happen and all will be perfect! It can't end badly.</span>
  <span id="freeText18185201526710380699" style="display:none">OHHHHHHH MYYYYYYYYYY GOOOOOOOOOOOOOOD! <br><br>WOW, JLA you never cease to amaze me with your awesomeness. I am so completely drained from this book. I am sick to my stomach and seriously am scared shitless for what's to come in Apollyon. But holy hell....that was freakin badass!<br><br><br>I am too tired and exhausted to write this review since my brain has been shut off. So I will stop here and leave you with...<br><br><br>TEAM AIDEX ALWAYS!!!!! I don't care, something will happen and all will be perfect! It can't end badly....please. My gods I love Aiden St Delphi....more than ever now!!!!<br><br>~Full review to come~<br><br><br><a href="http://s981.beta.photobucket.com/user/goddess793/library/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380366507i/718764._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Not even a day later and I am still sitting here trying to conjure up a good review for this fantastically epic book....and....nothing. More than likely it's due to my migraine that I've had for the good portion of this book because reading this I was all over the place, yelling and screaming and freaking out. IT WAS SO GOOD!<br><br>Anyway, so here goes nothing....<br><br>We leave off after Pure with Alex returning from New York and leaving some secrets behind that could destroy her and Aiden *sigh sigh sigh*. Upon returning, with the council still there, Alex has to figure out a way to keep quiet. Then she recieves a letter and in it is something that just adds onto her problems of crap. Poor girl, I swear she has been through hell and back. Anyway, when she finds out that Aiden has returned, she brings it to him for help as to how to solve THAT problem. I swear Aiden is the most chivalrous guy ever...so damn attentive and amazing. Sigh.<br><br>Sorry, Aiden makes me forget everything. I'll focus...focus. So now, the council returns to New York and Seth has to go and deal with some stuff there...thank you Seth for leaving you jerk off....stay gone! Things between them heat up and not in a good way. He is using the Akasha to channel Alex's power to gain more for himself because he's a selfish asshat. OMG, he pissed me off SOOOOOOOOOOOOO much in this book. I never was a fan of him from the beginning but he has crossed a line and I hate him more than ever! So yeah, he's become a puppet to someone and yeah maybe it's not his fault entirely but I don't think there is any coming back for him...which is good for Aiden because dammit he needs his happy ending. Seriously, Aiden and Alex are soul mates. I know Seth lovers will hate me and it's totally cool, I can take it. I don't like Seth. Never did and never will. But if there was a chance he could be saved...I hope he is and then leaves and never comes back. He has been a burden ever since he came into the picture...his bloodthirst for power has shown from the beginning. Honestly, I love my bad boys but Seth never once did anything for me, ever. Except make me want to vomit or punch a hole in my wall. So between her Awakening drawing nearer and Seth being an asshole and a liar and her stepdad being the evil fucktard and Aiden being the one she's always wanted but can't have, I'd say Alex Andros is really unlucky. Although we got so much STEAM....STEAM STEAM STEAM....holy Hell that was the BEST PART OF THIS WHOLE BOOK! I was glued to my nook and damn if I didn't drool all over myself....sweet Jesus I love the shit out of Aiden because he did things I have been waiting for him to do since Half-Blood and it brought tears to my eyes and joy to my heart. God, I know there is hope for them....there has to be. It can't end with....no it won't. I know I have to read Elixir and I am so on it. But seriously, this book is the best book so far of the series and honestly this series is by far my favorite JLA series and I am so feining for Apollyon right now. How the hell am I going to wait until the spring...I am literally dying now for it.<br><br>JLA never disappoints with her amazing stories and characters. This book proved that she can do no wrong, though I haven't finished Onyx I say this series is better than the Lux series. It was such a wild and thrilling and very emotionally draining rollercoaster. I was up and down and up and down and twisting every which way. I got to know more of the characters in this one so it was awesome! I loved Leon so much in this, he was so fecking funny! Also Deacon...gods I love that boy! He's just like his brother Aiden. Love them both so much. And Marcus....what can I say? He surprised me the most. Damn he's so awesome and I was happy to see how things turned out. There were some devastating parts and parts that left me speechless, breathless and ready to kick ass and take names! One thing I loved the most about this book (aside from Aiden of course) was the Greek mythology being thrown in there more. It was so intriguing and awesome! Loved it! Everything about this book had me reeling and so excited and crying and laughing....and feeling damn near every emotion in the world. Gods, this book was perfect! I really give Jen props for writing such a stellar continuation to a superb series. I am really excited and scared to see what happens next. With 2 more books coming out I can only imagine how Alex much more crazy shit Alex will have to endure. Seriously for a 17 year old she literally goes through the wringer...and I go right along for the ride, drained in the process...but I wouldn't have it any other way!<br><br>WELL DONE JENNIFER! WELL FREAKIN DONE!<br><br>Oh that ending....GODS THAT ENDING. I AM BITING MY NAILS FOR THE NEXT BOOK....I NEED IT! I FECKING NEEEEEEED IT! </span>

I need to know what she's going to be like in the next book now that she has awakened as an Apollyon. Seth is now likable to me because of his evil side. Aiden is adorable and I'm still sad that him and Alex haven't gotten married or had beautiful babies yet. <br /><br />I obviously ship Alex and Aiden together but after reading this book I'm so confused. HOW CAN I SHIP TWO PEOPLE TOGETHER WHEN JENNIFER KEEPS THEM APART?!?! Plus I just really want to know what's happening to Alex now. Like I said earlier, I can't accept that cliffhanger ending. <br /><br />I wish I had the next book but sadly it isn't available at my library... yet. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3306724600986599699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
